- `reviews-reproduced/doi_10.1190_1.1442147/` — Virieux 1986
  (the foundational P-SV velocity-stress staggered-grid paper;
  2nd-order in space, 2nd-order in time)
- `reviews-reproduced/doi_10.1190_1.1442422/` — Levander 1988
  (the 4th-order extension; "Fourth-order finite-difference P-SV
  seismograms")

Each folder is hermetically standalone (no cross-folder imports,
per `reviews-reproduced/CLAUDE.md` discipline). Each is pinned
to its own paper as the canonical reference:

- **Virieux 1986 folder** — the canonical claim is "this
  reproduces the 2nd-order stencil of Virieux's Eq 4". The
  folder's tests verify byte-match of the centred-FD stencil
  `[-1/2, 0, 1/2] / dx` at `so=2`, plus MMS convergence rate
  ≈ 2 at the same order. The driver also parametrises higher
  orders (`so ∈ {4, 8, 16}` per decision O) but those are
  documented as "higher-order extensions of the same scheme
  family — see Levander 1988 folder for the formal 4th-order
  claim".
- **Levander 1988 folder** — the canonical claim is "this
  reproduces the 4th-order stencil of Levander's Eq 4". Tests
  verify byte-match of `[1/24, -9/8, 9/8, -1/24] / dx` at
  `so=4`, plus MMS rate ≈ 4. Higher orders `so ∈ {8, 16}`
  exercised under decision O as "natural extensions" — flagged
  in test docstrings as "beyond the formal scope of Levander
  1988; included per repo-wide `so=16` convention".

Method 1's `reproduction_dois` becomes the tuple
`("doi_10.1190_1.1442147", "doi_10.1190_1.1442422")`.

Both reproductions share an architectural pattern (homogeneous
2D isotropic medium + Ricker source + reference wavefield
snapshot) but DUPLICATE the driver code per the standalone-
isolation discipline. The two drivers will look ~95% the same;
this is intentional. A future shared abstraction belongs upstream
in `devito-fd-survey/core/` (Phase 2b axis migration), NOT
crosswired between reproduction folders.

def _reproduction_root() -> Path:
    """Path to the `reproduced/` submodule root."""
    return REPO / "reproduced"


def test_reproduced_submodule_is_initialised():
    """Sanity check: the `reproduced/` submodule must be populated.

    A bare ``reproduced/`` directory (no checkout) means the
    submodule wasn't initialised after clone — run
    ``git submodule update --init --recursive``.
    """
    root = _reproduction_root()
    assert root.is_dir(), (
        f"Reproduced submodule directory missing at {root}. "
        f"Run `git submodule update --init --recursive` from the repo "
        f"root to populate it."
    )
    # The submodule must contain at least the methodology CLAUDE.md.
    claude_md = root / "CLAUDE.md"
    assert claude_md.is_file(), (
        f"Reproduced submodule appears uninitialised — {claude_md} "
        f"missing. Run `git submodule update --init --recursive`."
    )


def test_published_methods_have_reproduction_folders():
    """Per refactor round 4 gate: every published / novel-combination
    method MUST reference at least one reproduction folder via
    ``reproduction_dois``, and every referenced folder MUST exist.

    Methods in ``_PREREQUISITE_EXEMPT`` are skipped with a warning;
    the exemption is logged but does not fail the gate.
    """
    root = _reproduction_root()
    if not root.is_dir():
        pytest.skip("Reproduced submodule not initialised — see "
                    "test_reproduced_submodule_is_initialised")

    failures: list[str] = []
    warnings: list[str] = []
    for method_id, spec in METHOD_REGISTRY.items():
        if spec.provenance not in _REQUIRING_PROVENANCES:
            continue
        # Exempt methods are tracked but don't fail the gate.
        if method_id in _PREREQUISITE_EXEMPT:
            warnings.append(
                f"Method {method_id} ({spec.display_name}) "
                f"provenance='{spec.provenance}' is exempt: "
                f"{_PREREQUISITE_EXEMPT[method_id]}"
            )
            continue
        if not spec.reproduction_dois:
            failures.append(
                f"Method {method_id} ({spec.display_name}) is "
                f"provenance='{spec.provenance}' but "
                f"reproduction_dois is empty. Per refactor round 4 "
                f"gate: bootstrap a reviews-reproduced/doi_<DOI>/ "
                f"folder for each defining-feature paper first, "
                f"then wire reproduction_dois=(...) in the "
                f"registry. If this method is grandfathered, add "
                f"to _PREREQUISITE_EXEMPT in "
                f"tests/test_reproduction_prerequisites.py with a "
                f"tracking note."
            )
            continue
        for doi in spec.reproduction_dois:
            folder = root / doi
            if not folder.is_dir():
                failures.append(
                    f"Method {method_id} ({spec.display_name}) "
                    f"references reproduction folder "
                    f"reviews-reproduced/{doi}/ but the folder "
                    f"does not exist on disk (checked {folder}). "
                    f"Either bootstrap the folder OR fix the "
                    f"reproduction_dois entry."
                )
    # Surface warnings via stderr; do not fail.
    for w in warnings:
        print(w, file=sys.stderr)
    assert not failures, "\n".join(failures)


def test_reproduction_folders_have_required_files():
    """Per refactor round 4 gate: every reproduction folder
    referenced by a method MUST contain the canonical files:

    - ``pyproject.toml`` — uv-managed dependency pinning
    - ``run_reproduction.py`` — driver
    - ``tests/`` — standalone pytest subsuite
    - ``reference_outputs/`` — pinned reference outputs
    - ``README.md`` (or ``report.qmd``) — Devito implementation notes

    Exempt methods skipped.
    """
    root = _reproduction_root()
    if not root.is_dir():
        pytest.skip("Reproduced submodule not initialised")

    required_files = ("pyproject.toml", "run_reproduction.py")
    required_dirs = ("tests", "reference_outputs")

    failures: list[str] = []
    for method_id, spec in METHOD_REGISTRY.items():
        if spec.provenance not in _REQUIRING_PROVENANCES:
            continue
        if method_id in _PREREQUISITE_EXEMPT:
            continue
        for doi in spec.reproduction_dois:
            folder = root / doi
            if not folder.is_dir():
                continue   # caught by upstream test
            for fname in required_files:
                if not (folder / fname).is_file():
                    failures.append(
                        f"Method {method_id} reproduction folder "
                        f"reviews-reproduced/{doi}/ missing "
                        f"required file: {fname}"
                    )
            for dname in required_dirs:
                if not (folder / dname).is_dir():
                    failures.append(
                        f"Method {method_id} reproduction folder "
                        f"reviews-reproduced/{doi}/ missing "
                        f"required directory: {dname}/"
                    )

def _combine_verdicts(verdicts: list[str]) -> str:
    """AND-of-AGREE combinator: combined verdict is AGREE only if
    EVERY reviewer returned AGREE. Otherwise DISAGREE (if any
    reviewer DISAGREEd) or INCONCLUSIVE (if no DISAGREE but at
    least one INCONCLUSIVE).

    Conservative — the right bar for a literature-faithfulness gate.
    """
    if all(v == 'AGREE' for v in verdicts):
        return 'AGREE'
    if any(v == 'DISAGREE' for v in verdicts):
        return 'DISAGREE'
    return 'INCONCLUSIVE'


def _preflight_reproduction_prerequisites(method_id: int) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    """Pre-flight check (refactor round 4, 2026-05-25): a method with
    ``provenance ∈ {'published', 'novel-combination'}`` MUST have its
    defining-feature paper(s) reproduced under
    ``reviews-reproduced/doi_<DOI>/`` BEFORE the graduation review
    can be invoked.

    Skipped (with a warning) if the method appears in
    ``_PREREQUISITE_EXEMPT`` from
    ``tests/test_reproduction_prerequisites.py`` — Phase 7 cascade
    methods that pre-date the gate.

    Returns ``(ok, message)``.
    """
    repo_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
    spec = METHOD_REGISTRY[method_id]
    requiring = spec.provenance in ('published', 'novel-combination')
    if not requiring:
        return True, ''

    # Pull the exemption list lazily to avoid import cycles.
    try:
        sys.path.insert(0, str(repo_root / 'tests'))
        import test_reproduction_prerequisites as _gate
        exempt = _gate._PREREQUISITE_EXEMPT
    except Exception:
        exempt = {}
    finally:
        try:
            sys.path.remove(str(repo_root / 'tests'))
        except ValueError:
            pass

    if method_id in exempt:
        return True, (
            f"NOTE: Method {method_id} is on the reproduction "
            f"prerequisite exemption list ({exempt[method_id]}). "
            f"The graduation review can proceed but cannot graduate "
            f"the method to a permanent published claim until a "
            f"reproduction folder lands."
        )

    if not spec.reproduction_dois:
        return False, (
            f"Method {method_id} ({spec.display_name}) is "
            f"provenance='{spec.provenance}' but has no "
            f"reproduction_dois wired. Per refactor round 4 gate: "
            f"bootstrap a reviews-reproduced/doi_<DOI>/ folder for "
            f"each defining-feature paper first, then add "
            f"reproduction_dois=(...) to the registry entry. "
            f"Alternatively add to _PREREQUISITE_EXEMPT with a "
            f"tracking note."
        )

    reproduced_root = repo_root / 'reproduced'
    if not reproduced_root.is_dir():
        return False, (
            f"reviews-reproduced submodule is not initialised at "
            f"{reproduced_root}. Run "
            f"`git submodule update --init --recursive` first."
        )

    missing = []
    for doi in spec.reproduction_dois:
        folder = reproduced_root / doi
        if not folder.is_dir():
            missing.append(str(folder))
    if missing:
        return False, (
            f"Method {method_id} ({spec.display_name}) references "
            f"reproduction folder(s) that do not exist on disk:\n  "
            + "\n  ".join(missing)

def test_exempt_list_only_carries_published_methods():
    """Sanity check: every entry in _PREREQUISITE_EXEMPT must
    correspond to a method that is currently published /
    novel-combination. If a method drops to surrogate, it should
    be removed from the exemption list (the gate doesn't apply
    to surrogates).
    """
    failures: list[str] = []
    for method_id in _PREREQUISITE_EXEMPT:
        if method_id not in METHOD_REGISTRY:
            failures.append(
                f"_PREREQUISITE_EXEMPT references unknown method "
                f"{method_id}"
            )
            continue
        prov = METHOD_REGISTRY[method_id].provenance
        if prov not in _REQUIRING_PROVENANCES:
            failures.append(
                f"_PREREQUISITE_EXEMPT[{method_id}] but provenance "
                f"is '{prov}' — only published / novel-combination "
                f"methods need exemption. Remove this entry."
            )
    assert not failures, "\n".join(failures)
